		has_dlc = "The Cossacks"
		is_nomad = yes
		check_variable = {
			which = estate_tribals_weight_share

		NOT = {
			check_variable = {
				which = estate_tribals_loyalty

			has_country_modifier = tribes_demand_autonomy

	is_triggered_only = yes

		days = 1
	}

			}
		}
	}

			factor = 1

		hidden_effect = {

			}

					which = tribes_loyalty_removed

					}
